[Observation]
Contents of Assets/Scripts/NPC.cs:
```csharp
using UnityEngine;

[DisallowMultipleComponent]
public class NPC : MonoBehaviour
{
    [Header("Movement")]
    [SerializeField] private Transform[] _waypoints;
    [SerializeField, Min(0f)] private float _moveSpeed = 2f;
    [SerializeField, Min(0f)] private float _arrivalThreshold = 0.1f;

    private int _currentWaypointIndex;
    private int _direction = 1;

    private void FixedUpdate()
    {
        if (_waypoints == null || _waypoints.Length == 0)
        {
            return;
        }

        Transform targetWaypoint = _waypoints[_currentWaypointIndex];
        if (targetWaypoint == null)
        {
            AdvanceWaypointIndex();
            return;
        }

        Vector3 currentPosition = transform.position;
        Vector3 targetPosition = targetWaypoint.position;
        float step = _moveSpeed * Time.fixedDeltaTime;

        transform.position = Vector3.MoveTowards(currentPosition, targetPosition, step);

        if (Vector3.Distance(transform.position, targetPosition) <= _arrivalThreshold)
        {
            transform.position = targetPosition;
            AdvanceWaypointIndex();
        }
    }

    private void AdvanceWaypointIndex()
    {
        if (_waypoints == null || _waypoints.Length == 0)
        {
            return;
        }

        int nextIndex = _currentWaypointIndex + _direction;

        if (nextIndex >= _waypoints.Length)
        {
            _direction = -1;
            nextIndex = _waypoints.Length > 1 ? _waypoints.Length - 2 : 0;
        }
        else if (nextIndex < 0)
        {
            _direction = 1;
            nextIndex = _waypoints.Length > 1 ? 1 : 0;
        }

        _currentWaypointIndex = Mathf.Clamp(nextIndex, 0, _waypoints.Length - 1);
    }

    private void OnMouseDown()
    {
        Debug.Log("NPC clicked");
    }
}

```
